for pingcap/tidb v8.5.0\\n\\n### 1. PrivilegeManager Interface\\n\\n**File: `pkg/privilege/privilege.go`**\\n\\nThis file defines the central `Manager` interface (the PrivilegeManager interface). It declares all privilege-related operations:\\n- `RequestVerification(activeRole []*auth.RoleIdentity, db, table, column string, priv mysql.PrivilegeType) bool` \u2014 checks static (table/db/global) privileges for the current session user.\\n- `RequestVerificationWithUser(...)` \u2014 checks static privileges for a specific user (used for view SECURITY DEFINER checks).\\n- `RequestDynamicVerification(activeRoles, privName, grantable)` \u2014 checks dynamic (named) privileges like BACKUP_ADMIN, ROLE_ADMIN, etc.\\n- `RequestDynamicVerificationWithUser(...)` \u2014 dynamic privilege check for a specific user.\\n- `HasExplicitlyGrantedDynamicPrivilege(...)` \u2014 checks dynamic privilege without SUPER fallback.\\n- `ConnectionVerification(...)` \u2014 verifies user credentials at connection time.\\n- `ShowGrants(...)`, `ActiveRoles(...)`, `FindEdge(...)`, `GetDefaultRoles(...)`, `GetAllRoles(...)`, `DBIsVisible(...)`, `UserPrivilegesTable(...)`, `IsDynamicPrivilege(...)`, `MatchIdentity(...)`, etc.\\n\\n`BindPrivilegeManager` and `GetPrivilegeManager` bind/retrieve the Manager from the session context.\\n\\n### 2. MySQLPrivilege Cache\\n\\n**File: `pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go`**\\n\\nThis is the largest and most critical file. It contains:\\n\\n- **`MySQLPrivilege` struct**: The in-memory cache of all MySQL privilege tables. It embeds `immutable` (slices of `UserRecord`, `dbRecord`, `tablesPrivRecord`, `columnsPrivRecord`, `defaultRoleRecord`, `globalPrivRecord`, `dynamicPrivRecord`, and `roleGraph map[string]roleGraphEdgesTable`) and `extended` (hash maps for fast lookup: `UserMap`, `DBMap`, `TablesPrivMap`, `Global`, `Dynamic`).\\n\\n- **`Handle` struct**: Wraps `MySQLPrivilege` with an `atomic.Pointer` for lock-free reads. `Handle.Get()` returns the current snapshot; `Handle.Update()` reloads all privilege tables from storage; `Handle.ensureActiveUser()` lazily loads a specific user's data.\\n\\n- **SQL load queries**: Constants like `sqlLoadRoleGraph`, `sqlLoadUserTable`, `sqlLoadDBTable`, `sqlLoadTablePrivTable`, `sqlLoadColumnsPrivTable`, `sqlLoadGlobalGrantsTable`, `sqlLoadDefaultRoles` define the queries used to populate the cache from `mysql.*` system tables.\\n\\n- **`LoadAll` / `LoadRoleGraph`**: Load all privilege data or just the role graph from the database into the in-memory cache.\\n\\n- **`RequestVerification`** (on `MySQLPrivilege`): The core privilege check. It calls `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles` to expand the user's active roles (including inherited roles via BFS), then checks user-level, db-level, table-level, and column-level privilege records in order, returning true if any level grants the requested privilege.\\n\\n- **`RequestDynamicVerification`** / **`HasExplicitlyGrantedDynamicPrivilege`**: Check dynamic (named) privileges from `mysql.global_grants`, with SUPER privilege as a fallback for `RequestDynamicVerification`.\\n\\n- **`matchUser`, `matchDB`, `matchTables`, `matchColumns`**: Pattern-matching helpers that find the best-matching privilege record for a given user/host/db/table/column combination.\\n\\n- **`showGrants`** / **`UserPrivilegesTable`**: Generate SHOW GRANTS output and INFORMATION_SCHEMA.USER_PRIVILEGES rows.\\n\\n- **`connectionVerification`**: Finds the user record for connection authentication.\\n\\n### 3. Role Graph Resolution Logic\\n\\n**File: `pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go`**\\n\\n- **`roleGraphEdgesTable`**: Stores the set of roles granted to a user/role as a `map[string]*auth.RoleIdentity`. The `Find(user, host)` method checks if a specific role is in the set.\\n\\n- **`decodeRoleEdgesTable`**: Decodes rows from `mysql.role_edges` into the `roleGraph` map (keyed by `toUser@toHost`, value is the set of roles granted to that user).\\n\\n- **`LoadRoleGraph`**: Loads the entire `mysql.role_edges` table into `p.roleGraph`.\\n\\n- **`FindRole(user, host, role)`**: Checks if there is a direct edge between a user and a role in the role graph.\\n\\n- **`FindAllRole(activeRoles)`**: Performs a **breadth-first search** (BFS) over the role graph starting from the given active roles, returning all transitively reachable roles. This implements role inheritance.\\n\\n- **`FindAllUserEffectiveRoles(user, host, activeRoles)`**: Filters `activeRoles` to only those actually granted to the user (via `FindRole`), then calls `FindAllRole` for BFS expansion. This is called at the start of every `RequestVerification` call.\\n\\n- **`UserPrivileges.ActiveRoles`** (in `privileges.go`): Called when a session activates roles (`SET ROLE`); validates that each role in the list is actually granted to the user.\\n\\n### 4. RequestVerification Method and Its Callers\\n\\n**Primary implementation**: `MySQLPrivilege.RequestVerification` in `pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go` (line 1333).\\n\\n**Manager-level wrapper**: `UserPrivileges.RequestVerification` in `pkg/privilege/privileges/privileges.go` (line 142). This wrapper:\\n1. Short-circuits if `SkipWithGrant` is set.\\n2. Applies SEM (Security Enhanced Mode) restrictions \u2014 blocks writes to system tables and hides invisible tables for users without `RESTRICTED_TABLES_ADMIN`.\\n3. Calls extension access check functions.\\n4. Delegates to `MySQLPrivilege.RequestVerification`.\\n5. Optionally calls an auth-plugin-provided verification function.\\n\\n**Callers of `RequestVerification` / `GetPrivilegeManager`**:\\n- `pkg/planner/core/optimizer.go`: `CheckPrivilege` \u2014 the main privilege enforcement point, called after plan building.\\n- `pkg/planner/core/logical_plan_builder.go`: View SECURITY DEFINER check and EXPLAIN privilege check.\\n- `pkg/planner/core/preprocess.go`: Early check during preprocessing \u2014 if a table doesn't exist, checks whether the user has any privilege on it before revealing the error.\\n- `pkg/planner/core/point_get_plan.go`: Privilege check for point-get fast path plans.\\n- `pkg/planner/core/plan_cache.go`: Privilege re-check when executing a cached prepared statement.\\n- `pkg/planner/optimize.go`: Main `optimize` function calls `CheckPrivilege` after building the logical plan; also checks `RESOURCE_GROUP_ADMIN`/`RESOURCE_GROUP_USER` for resource group hints.\\n- `pkg/expression/sessionexpr/sessionctx.go`: `EvalContext.RequestVerification` \u2014 used by built-in functions (e.g., sequence functions, `current_user()`, `tidb_decode_plan()`) that need privilege checks during expression evaluation.\\n- `pkg/planner/core/expression_codec_fn.go`: Uses `PrivilegeChecker.RequestVerification` for codec functions accessing partitioned tables.\\n- `pkg/executor/infoschema_reader.go`: Filters INFORMATION_SCHEMA rows based on per-table/per-schema privileges.\\n- `pkg/session/session.go`: Various session-level checks (e.g., checking table access for stale reads, checking privileges for `USE db`).\\n- `pkg/infoschema/cluster.go`, `pkg/infoschema/tables.go`: Cluster-level information schema privilege filtering.\\n- `pkg/server/conn.go`: Connection-level privilege checks (e.g., killing connections).\\n- `pkg/ddl/executor.go`: DDL executor privilege checks.\\n- `pkg/executor/import_into.go`: IMPORT INTO privilege checks.\\n\\n### 5. Files That Map SQL Statement Types to Required Privileges\\n\\n**File: `pkg/planner/core/planbuilder.go`**\\n\\nThis is the primary file mapping SQL AST node types to required privileges via the `visitInfo` mechanism. The `PlanBuilder.Build` method dispatches to statement-specific builders:\\n\\n- **`buildSimple`** (line 3562): Maps simple statements to privileges:\\n  - `FlushStmt` \u2192 `RELOAD`\\n  - `AlterInstanceStmt` \u2192 `SUPER`\\n  - `RenameUserStmt` \u2192 `CREATE USER`\\n  - `GrantStmt` \u2192 delegates to `collectVisitInfoFromGrantStmt`\\n  - `BRIEStmt` (BACKUP/RESTORE) \u2192 `BACKUP_ADMIN` / `RESTORE_ADMIN` (dynamic)\\n  - `CalibrateResourceStmt`, `AddQueryWatchStmt`, `DropQueryWatchStmt` \u2192 `RESOURCE_GROUP_ADMIN`\\n  - `GrantRoleStmt`, `RevokeRoleStmt` \u2192 `ROLE_ADMIN`\\n  - `KillStmt` \u2192 `CONNECTION_ADMIN` (if killing another user's connection)\\n  - `ShutdownStmt` \u2192 `SHUTDOWN`\\n  - `SetResourceGroupStmt` \u2192 `RESOURCE_GROUP_ADMIN` or `RESOURCE_GROUP_USER`\\n  - `RevokeStmt` \u2192 delegates to `collectVisitInfoFromRevokeStmt`\\n\\n- **`buildDDL`** (line 4965): Maps DDL statements:\\n  - `AlterDatabaseStmt` \u2192 `ALTER` on db\\n  - `AlterTableStmt` \u2192 `ALTER` on table; `DROP`/`CREATE`/`INSERT` for RENAME/EXCHANGE PARTITION; `DROP` for DROP PARTITION; `REFERENCES` for FK constraints\\n  - `CreateDatabaseStmt` \u2192 `CREATE` on db\\n  - `CreateIndexStmt` \u2192 `INDEX` on table\\n  - `CreateTableStmt` \u2192 `CREATE` on table (or `CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE` for local temp tables); `REFERENCES` for FK\\n  - `CreateViewStmt` \u2192 `CREATE VIEW`; `SUPER` if definer differs from current user\\n  - `CreateSequenceStmt` \u2192 `CREATE`\\n  - `DropDatabaseStmt` \u2192 `DROP` on db\\n  - `DropIndexStmt` \u2192 `INDEX`\\n  - `DropTableStmt`, `DropSequenceStmt`, `TruncateTableStmt` \u2192 `DROP`\\n  - `RenameTableStmt` \u2192 `ALTER` + `DROP` on old table, `CREATE` + `INSERT` on new table\\n  - `RecoverTableStmt`, `FlashBackTableStmt` \u2192 `CREATE` + `DROP`\\n  - `FlashBackDatabaseStmt` \u2192 `CREATE` + `DROP` on db\\n  - `FlashBackToTimestampStmt` \u2192 `SUPER`\\n  - `LockTablesStmt` \u2192 `LOCK TABLES` + `SELECT`\\n  - `CleanupTableLockStmt`, `RepairTableStmt` \u2192 `SUPER`\\n  - `DropPlacementPolicyStmt`, `CreatePlacementPolicyStmt`, `AlterPlacementPolicyStmt` \u2192 `PLACEMENT_ADMIN`\\n  - `CreateResourceGroupStmt`, `DropResourceGroupStmt`, `AlterResourceGroupStmt` \u2192 `RESOURCE_GROUP_ADMIN`\\n\\n- **`buildShow`** (line 3393): Maps SHOW statements:\\n  - `ShowCreateTable` (non-view) \u2192 `AllPrivMask`; (view) \u2192 `SHOW VIEW`\\n  - `ShowCreateView` \u2192 `SELECT` + `SHOW VIEW`\\n  - `ShowConfig` \u2192 `CONFIG`\\n  - `ShowBackups` \u2192 `BACKUP_ADMIN`; `ShowRestores` \u2192 `RESTORE_ADMIN`\\n  - `ShowTableNextRowId` \u2192 `SELECT`\\n  - `ShowStatsExtended`, `ShowStatsHealthy`, etc. \u2192 `SELECT` on `mysql` system db\\n  - `ShowStatsBuckets`, `ShowStatsHistograms`, `ShowStatsMeta`, `ShowStatsLocked` \u2192 `SELECT` on table\\n\\n- **`buildInsert`** (line 3885): `INSERT` privilege; additionally `DELETE` for REPLACE INTO, `UPDATE` for ON DUPLICATE KEY UPDATE.\\n\\n- **`buildAnalyze`** (line 3099): `INSERT` + `SELECT` via `requireInsertAndSelectPriv`.\\n\\n- **`buildLoadData`** (line 4358): `INSERT`; additionally `DELETE` for REPLACE mode.\\n\\n- **`buildImportInto`** (line 4516): `INSERT` on target table; SELECT privileges on source tables if using SELECT subquery.\\n\\n- **`buildAdmin`** (line 1474): All ADMIN commands require `SUPER`.\\n\\n- **`collectVisitInfoFromGrantStmt`** (line 3751): For GRANT statements, requires the privileges being granted plus `GRANT OPTION`.\\n\\n- **`collectVisitInfoFromRevokeStmt`** (line 3687): For REVOKE statements, requires the privileges being revoked plus `GRANT OPTION`.\\n\\n- **`appendVisitInfoIsRestrictedUser`** (line 3739): When SEM is enabled, checks if the target user has `RESTRICTED_USER_ADMIN` and if so requires the caller to also have it.\\n\\n**File: `pkg/planner/core/logical_plan_builder.go`**\\n\\n- **`buildSelect`** (line 3680): Adds `SELECT` privilege for each table referenced in the FROM clause (line 4398). For views with SECURITY DEFINER, directly calls `pm.RequestVerificationWithUser` to check the definer's privileges.\\n- **`buildUpdate`** (line 5471): Adds `UPDATE` privilege for each column being updated (line 5859).\\n- **`buildDelete`** (line 5890): Adds `DELETE` privilege for each table being deleted from (lines 6011, 6035).\\n- **`appendVisitInfo`** (line 7105): Appends a static privilege requirement to the visitInfo list.\\n- **`appendDynamicVisitInfo`** (line 7096): Appends a dynamic privilege requirement (using `mysql.ExtendedPriv` sentinel).\\n\\n**File: `pkg/planner/core/optimizer.go`**\\n\\n- **`CheckPrivilege`** (line 126): Iterates the `visitInfo` list. For each entry with `mysql.ExtendedPriv`, calls `pm.RequestDynamicVerification` for each dynamic privilege (OR semantics). For static privileges, calls `pm.RequestVerification`. Returns an error if any check fails.\\n- **`VisitInfo4PrivCheck`** (line 155): Adjusts visitInfo for local temporary tables \u2014 `CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE` requires `CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE` privilege from the db scope, and subsequent DML on local temp tables requires no privileges.\\n\\n**File: `pkg/planner/optimize.go`**\\n\\n- **`optimize`** (line 465): After building the logical plan, calls `core.VisitInfo4PrivCheck` then `core.CheckPrivilege` to enforce all collected privilege requirements. This is the main enforcement point in the query execution pipeline.\\n\\n### 6. Supporting Files\\n\\n- **`pkg/expression/expropt/priv.go`**: Defines the `PrivilegeChecker` interface used by expression evaluation (a simplified version of `Manager` without active roles). `PrivilegeCheckerProvider` and `PrivilegeCheckerPropReader` integrate it into the expression evaluation context system.\\n\\n- **`pkg/expression/sessionexpr/sessionctx.go`**: `EvalContext.RequestVerification` and `EvalContext.RequestDynamicVerification` implement `PrivilegeChecker` by delegating to `privilege.GetPrivilegeManager`.\\n\\n- **`pkg/parser/mysql/privs.go`**: Defines `PrivilegeType` (uint64 bitmask), all privilege constants (`SelectPriv`, `InsertPriv`, etc.), `AllGlobalPrivs`, `AllDBPrivs`, `AllTablePrivs`, `AllPrivMask`, `Priv2Str`, `Priv2UserCol` (maps privilege types to `mysql.user` column names), and `Col2PrivType`.\\n\\n- **`pkg/privilege/privileges/errors.go`**: Defines privilege-specific errors: `ErrAccessDenied`, `ErrNonexistingGrant`, `errLoadPrivilege`, `ErrMustChangePasswordLogin`, etc.\\n\\n- **`pkg/privilege/privileges/tidb_auth_token.go`**: Implements TiDB auth token (JWT-based) authentication plugin.\\n\\n- **`pkg/privilege/privileges/ldap/`**: LDAP authentication plugins (simple and SASL variants) used as auth backends.\\n\\n- **`pkg/privilege/conn/conn.go`**: Defines `AuthConn` interface for auth plugin \u2194 client communication during connection establishment.\\n\\n### 7. Privilege Check Flow Summary\\n\\n1. **SQL parsing** produces an AST node.\\n2. **`PlanBuilder.Build`** dispatches to a statement-specific builder (`buildSelect`, `buildInsert`, `buildDDL`, `buildSimple`, etc.).\\n3. Each builder calls `appendVisitInfo` or `appendDynamicVisitInfo` to record the required privilege(s) for each table/db/column accessed.\\n4. **`pkg/planner/optimize.go:optimize`** calls `VisitInfo4PrivCheck` (adjusts for temp tables) then `CheckPrivilege`.\\n5. **`CheckPrivilege`** in `pkg/planner/core/optimizer.go` iterates the visitInfo list and calls `pm.RequestVerification` (static) or `pm.RequestDynamicVerification` (dynamic) on the `Manager`.\\n6. **`UserPrivileges.RequestVerification`** in `pkg/privilege/privileges/privileges.go` applies SEM restrictions, extension checks, then delegates to `MySQLPrivilege.RequestVerification`.\\n7. **`MySQLPrivilege.RequestVerification`** in `pkg/privilege/privileges/cache.go` calls `FindAllUserEffectiveRoles` to expand active roles via BFS over the role graph, then checks user \u2192 db \u2192 table \u2192 column privilege records in order.\\n8. For **dynamic privileges**, `MySQLPrivilege.RequestDynamicVerification` checks `mysql.global_grants` records, with SUPER+GRANT_OPTION as a fallback.\\n9. **Connection-time** privilege checks use `UserPrivileges.ConnectionVerification` \u2192 `MySQLPrivilege.connectionVerification` to authenticate users against `mysql.user`.\"\n}\n",
